  var STYLE_ID = 'at-body-style';
  function getParent() {
    return doc.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
  }
  function addStyle(parent, id, def) {
    if (!parent) {
      return;
    }
    var style = doc.createElement('style');
    style.id = id;
    style.innerHTML = def;
    parent.appendChild(style);
  }

    if (!parent) {

      return;
    }

    <div class="banner-wrapper">
     <div class="container-fluid">
            <div class="row">
                        <div class="col-12 d-flex justify-content-center">
                            <span class="rc-type">Research Reports</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                <div class="row justify-content-center">
                    <div class="col-12 col-lg-10">
                        <h1 class="page-heading"> 2023 Unit 42 Ransomware and Extortion Report</h1>
                        </div>
             </div>

             <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-12 stats-widget">
                            <div class="col-block" style="display: none;">
                                    <div class="resourceDownloadBar downloadBar baseComponent parbase"></div>
</div>
                            <div class="byline-section col-block">
                            <div class="byline baseComponent parbase"><span>
          Mar 21, 2023</span>
      </div>
</div>
                    </div>
             </div>
            <div class="row justify-content-center">
                    <div class="col-12 col-xl-10">
                            <div class="content-section">
                               <div class="col-12 col-sm-4">
                                        <div class="document-block ">
                                            <figure class="">
                                                                <img src="/content/dam/pan/en_US/assets/pdf/reports/2023-unit42-ransomware-extortion-report.pdf.transform/globalsitesDocListThumb/image.png" alt="asset thumbnail" width="143" height="189" nolozad="true"/>
                                                            </figure>
                                                        </div>
                                          <!-- code section for download and preview button below resource icon -->
                                          <!-- end of code section for download and preview button below resource icon -->
                                    </div>
                                
                                <div class="content col-sm-8">
                                    <div class="secureParsys parsys"><div class="text baseComponent parbase section"><p>Approximately 50% of ransomware attacks and breaches fielded by the Unit 42<sup>®</sup> Incident Response team result from a common culprit: attack surface exposures.</p>
<p>Ransomware is no longer simply about encrypting files and asking for Bitcoin. New harassment tactics and double and triple extortion make the traditional advice about maintaining backups insufficient. Organizations need to be prepared for the latest techniques used by modern-day ransomware gangs, requiring a more in-depth incident response plan to achieve ransomware resilience. For example, the Unit 42 Incident Response team saw data theft in about 70% of ransomware incidents involving negotiations (up from about 40% in mid-2021).</p>
<p>Download the “2023 Unit 42 Ransomware and Extortion Report” to truly understand the threats you face, including.</p>
<ul>
<li>Ransomware and extortion trends and predictions.</li>
<li>Most-targeted industries.</li>
<li>Why having backups is no longer enough.</li>
<li>Best practices to protect your organization.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

	<!-- verifyEmail:
		This is the landing screen after a user clicks on the link in the
		verification email sent to the user when they've registered with a
		non-verified email address.

		HOW IT WORKS: The code that is generated by Capture and included in the
		link sent in the verification email is sent to the server and, if valid,
		the user's email will be marked as valid and the verifyEmailSuccess
		screen will be rendered. If the code is not accepted for any reason,
		the verifyEmail screen is shown and the user has another opportunity
		to have the verification email sent to them.

		NOTE: The links generated in the emails sent to users are based on
		Capture settings found in Janrain's Capture Dashboard. In addition to
		entering the URL of your email verification page, you will need to add
		'screenToRender' as a parameter in the URL with a value of 'verifyEmail'
		which is this screen.
	-->
